        const fpPromise = FingerprintJS.load();

            .then(fp => fp.get())
            .then(result => {

    <script src="https://www.classifieds.co.zw/js/search.js" type="5e9472fa9f03de20480e0404-text/javascript"></script>

    <script type="5e9472fa9f03de20480e0404-text/javascript">
        var filtersLimit = 7;
        var searchesUrl = "";
        var savedSearchesUrl = "?app_domain=classifieds.co.zw";

        $('[id^=cat-]').change(function() {
            var parent = $(this).attr('data-parentCat');
            if ($(this).is(':checked')) {
                $('#cat-' + parent).prop('checked', false);
                $('[data-parentCat=' + $(this).val() + "]").prop('checked', false);
            }
        });

        $('[id^=loc-]').change(function() {
            var parent = $(this).attr('data-parentLoc');
            if ($(this).is(':checked')) {
                $('#loc-' + parent).prop('checked', false);
                var myId = $(this).attr('id').substr(4);
                $('[data-parentLoc=' + myId + "]").prop('checked', false);
            }
        });

        jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
            $("#select-order").prop("disabled", false);
        });
    </script>

<script src="/js/custom-select.js?id=faac7b862d4f25512ab8" type="5e9472fa9f03de20480e0404-text/javascript"></script>
